## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics (nonlinear oscillators)
**Analysis**: The target dv_dt is acceleration expressed as a function of position x, velocity v, and possibly time t, which is the standard state-space form of (non)linear second-order oscillators. Common physics includes nonlinear restoring forces (spring/potential), velocity-dependent damping, and optional periodic/parametric external forcing in time.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Undamped linear oscillator (Hooke restoring): dv_dt = -c0 * x (mass-spring with no damping/forcing)
- Linear viscous damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v (damped harmonic oscillator)
- Constant acceleration bias: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v + c2 (gravity/bias or equilibrium offset in acceleration)
- Nonlinear spring (Duffing, cubic stiffness): dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * v (hardening/softening spring with damping)
- Higher-order restoring (polynomial potential): dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * x**5 - c3 * v (strong nonlinearity at large amplitude)
- Pendulum-type restoring: dv_dt = -c0 * sin(c1 * x) - c2 * v (geometric nonlinearity with viscous damping)
- Saturating restoring force: dv_dt = -c0 * tanh(c1 * x) - c2 * v (restoring force saturates for large |x|)
- Quadratic/aerodynamic damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * Abs(v) * v (drag proportional to v|v|)
- Nonlinear (cubic) damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v - c2 * v**3 (amplitude-dependent dissipation)
- Dry-friction-like regularization: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v - c2 * v / (Abs(v) + c3) (Coulomb friction smoothed near v=0)
- Van der Pol (self-excited) oscillator: dv_dt = -c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (negative damping at small |x|, positive at large |x|)
- General Liénard form: dv_dt = -c0 * g(x) - c1 * f(x) * v (broad class where restoring g(x) and damping f(x) depend on x)
- Additive periodic forcing: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v + c2 * cos(c3 * t) (externally driven oscillator)
- Harmonic forcing with phase mix: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v + c2 * cos(c3 * t) + c4 * sin(c3 * t) (equivalent to single sinusoid with phase)
- Parametric excitation (time-varying stiffness): dv_dt = -(c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x - c3 * v (Mathieu-type parametric resonance)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Conservative restoring force from a potential implies dv_dt depends primarily on x (and not on v or t), often as an odd function of x around equilibrium (e.g., -x, -x - x^3, -sin(x)).
- Viscous dissipation typically appears as a term proportional to -v; additional nonlinear drag appears as -Abs(v)*v or -v**3, indicating stronger damping at high speeds.
- Self-excited/limit-cycle behavior is suggested by damping that changes sign with amplitude, e.g., (1 - c * x**2) * v, producing energy injection at small |x| and dissipation at large |x|.
- External periodic driving is indicated by additive sinusoids in t (cos(c*t), sin(c*t)); resonance behavior often couples with the linear restoring frequency scale.
- Parametric resonance is indicated by time-dependent stiffness multiplying x, e.g., (c0 + c1*cos(c2*t)) * x, rather than additive forcing.
- Symmetry: if the physical oscillator is symmetric about x=0, expect dv_dt to be odd in x and odd in v for damping (no even-power x terms unless equilibrium is shifted).
- Hardening vs softening springs correspond to the sign of the x**3 term in dv_dt (positive cubic stiffness tends to increase frequency with amplitude; negative decreases it).
- Stick-slip or dry friction can manifest as near-discontinuous dependence on v; smooth rational approximations like v/(Abs(v)+c) often fit data better than sharp sign(v) in regression.

Best expression     : c0*x + c1 + c2*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*x/(c6*x**2 + 1) + c7*tanh(c8*x + c9)
Structure desc      : Additive model combining a dominant linear-in-x term, a time-only sinusoid, an x-dependent rational term x/(1+c6 x^2), and a shifted/scaled tanh nonlinearity. x appears in three places (linear, rational, tanh) while t appears only inside sin; there is no x–t interaction. With c3≈1 and c4≈π, the sinusoid is essentially a phase-flipped sin(t) with modest amplitude (~0.5), whereas c0=-19.5 makes the linear trend in x large; the rational term behaves ~12.49x for small x but decays like ~41.5/x for large |x|, and the tanh term (c7=7.12, c8=-2.35, c9=-3.79) acts like an x-dependent step offset switching near x≈-1.61. Approximate simplification: y ≈ -19.5x + 6.05 + 0.5·sin(t) + 7.12·tanh(-2.35x-3.79) + 12.49x/(1+0.301x^2) (with the last two terms saturating/decaying for large |x|).

GT Equivalence Verification (PO40)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*Abs(v)**c0 - omega0**c1*(gamma*Abs(v)**c2 + c3)*x - omega0**c4*x**c5 - omega0**c6*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fully numeric) is
\[
F(x,t,v)= -3.39285482994202\,x^3\;-\;3.39285482994202\,x\big(0.0780638344630251\,|v|^{1/3}+1\big)\;-\;3.39285482994202\,x\;+\;0.523287159969136\sin(t)\;-\;0.710540944238196\,|v|^{1/3}.
\]
So GT contains **(i)** a pure \(x^3\) term, **(ii)** linear-in-\(x\) terms, **(iii)** a forcing term proportional to \(\sin(t)\), and crucially **(iv)** non-polynomial damping terms involving \(|v|^{1/3}\) and also an \(x|v|^{1/3}\) coupling. Any globally equivalent candidate must be able to represent \(|v|^{1/3}\) dependence (and the \(x|v|^{1/3}\) product) exactly; rational-in-\(x\), tanh-in-\(x\), \(v^2\), \(v^3\), etc. cannot equal \(|v|^{1/3}\) for all real \(v\).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether it has the necessary functional forms; if not, no choice of constants can fix that.

---

### Candidates 1–5 (sin(t) + rational/tanh in x; no v dependence)
1. \(c0 x + c1 + c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+ c5 \frac{x}{c6 x^2+1}+ c7\tanh(c8 x+c9)\)  
   Has no \(v\) at all, but GT depends on \(|v|^{1/3}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot match.

2. Similar to (1) but with \(x^3/(c6 x^2+1)\). Still no \(v\). Cannot match.

3–5 similarly have no \(v\). Cannot match.

---

### Candidates 6–7 (polynomials in v, exp(t), v*sin)
6. \(c0 x + c1 + c2 v^2 + c3 v^2 x e^{c4 t} + c5 v\sin(c6 t+c7)\)  
   Uses \(v^2\) and \(v\sin(\cdot)\), not \(|v|^{1/3}\). Also introduces \(e^{c4 t}\) unless \(c3=0\). Even if you zero unwanted terms, you cannot create \(|v|^{1/3}\) or \(x|v|^{1/3}\). No match.

7. Same issue: only \(v^2\) terms. No match.

---

### Candidates 8–17 (x^3 possible, sin(t) possible, but v missing)
8–17 are combinations of \(x\), \(x^3\), \(\sin(\cdot)\), rational-in-\(x\), tanh-in-\(x\), constants. None include \(v\).  
GT has essential \(|v|^{1/3}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\). Therefore 8–17 cannot match.

(Trigonometric note: many have \(\sin(c3 t+c4)\), which could match \(\sin(t)\) by setting \(c3=1,c4=0\) (or phase-shift variants), but the missing \(v\)-dependence already blocks equivalence.)

---

### Candidate 18 (x + sin + x^3 only)
18. \(c0 x + c1 + c2\sin(c3 t+c4) + c5 x^3\)  
No \(v\). Cannot match.

---

### Candidate 19 (adds \(x(c7+v)^{c8}\) but no Abs and wrong structure)
19. \(c0 x + c1 + c2\sin(c3 t+c4) + c5 x^3 + c6 x(c7+v)^{c8}\)

Could we force \((c7+v)^{c8}\) to equal \(|v|^{1/3}\)? Problems:
- GT uses \(|v|^{1/3}\), which is **even** in \(v\) and non-analytic at 0; \((c7+v)^{c8}\) without Abs is not equal to \(|v|^{1/3}\) on all real \(v\) for any real constants (it changes sign/complex for negative \(c7+v\) when \(c8=1/3\)).  
- Also GT needs both a standalone \(-0.7105|v|^{1/3}\) term and an \(x|v|^{1/3}\) term. Candidate 19 can only produce an \(x\cdot f(v)\) term, not a standalone \(f(v)\) term.
So no match.

---

### Candidates 20–43 (mostly \(v^2\), exp(|t|)cos, other nonmatching forms)
20–43 all share the core structure \(c0 x + c1 v^2 + c2 v^2 x + c3 e^{c4|t|}\cos(c5 t) + \dots\) with various extra terms.

Key mismatches versus GT:
- GT has \(|v|^{1/3}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\), not \(v^2\) or \(v^2 x\). No constant choice makes \(v^2\equiv |v|^{1/3}\) for all real \(v\).
- GT has \(\sin(t)\), not \(e^{c4|t|}\cos(c5 t)\). You could try \(c4=0\) to remove the exponential and then use a phase shift to convert cos to sin (cos(\(t-\pi/2\)) = sin(t)), but these candidates use **cos**, not sin; still phase shift can handle that if \(c4=0\) and \(c5=1\). However the \(v\)-dependence mismatch remains fatal.
- Extra terms like \(x^{c7}e^{c8 x}\), \(e^{c7 x^2}\), \(v\cos(c7 t)|v|\), \(v/(c7+|v|)\), \(x(c7+v)^{c8}\), etc. cannot be tuned to become exactly \(|v|^{1/3}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\) simultaneously while also matching the exact polynomial-in-\(x\) structure.

Thus 20–43: no match.

(Quick specifics where tempting:)
- 37 has \(v\cos(c7 t)\,|v|\) which is \(|v|v\cos(\cdot)\), still not \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 40 has \(v/(c7+|v|)\), bounded; cannot equal unbounded \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 41/43 have \(x(c7+x)^{c8}\) or \(x(c7+v)^{c8}\) but again no standalone \(|v|^{1/3}\) term and no Abs on the power.

---

### Candidates 44–50 (logs, exp(t)sin(x+...), v^2 terms)
44. Includes \(\log(c8|v|+1)\) inside products of logs; not \(|v|^{1/3}\). No.

45. Has \(\sin(c7\log(c8|v|+1)+c9)\); oscillatory in \(\log|v|\), cannot equal \(|v|^{1/3}\). No.

46. Has \(e^{c7|v|}/x^2\) and \(v^2 e^{c3 t}\sin(c4 x+c5)\); wrong dependence and singular in \(x\). No.

47–48–50: contain \(v^2 x\) and \(e^{c3 t}\sin(c4 x+c5)\) plus cos/exp(sin)/exp(t)sin terms; none can produce \(|v|^{1/3}\) or \(x|v|^{1/3}\) and they introduce \(x\)-inside-sine which GT does not have. No.

49. Has \(v^2\) and \(v^2 x\) and \(t(c7+x)^{c8}\); no \(|v|^{1/3}\). No.

---

### Conclusion
Every candidate either (a) has **no \(v\)** at all, or (b) has \(v\) only through \(v^2\), \(v^3\), rational forms, exponentials, logs, or \((v+c)^{p}\) without Abs, none of which can be made globally identical to the GT’s required \(|v|^{1/3}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\) terms for all real \(v\) (with negative values allowed). Therefore no candidate can be parameter-tuned to equal the fixed GT function.

**GT numerical expression:**
`-3.39285482994202*x**3 - 3.39285482994202*x*(0.0780638344630251*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 3.39285482994202*x + 0.523287159969136*sin(t) - 0.710540944238196*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333`

Let me expand this:
- `-3.39285482994202*x**3`
- `-3.39285482994202*x*0.0780638344630251*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 - 3.39285482994202*x`
- `-3.39285482994202*x`
- `+0.523287159969136*sin(t)`
- `-0.710540944238196*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333`

Combining x terms: `-3.39285482994202*x - 3.39285482994202*x = -6.78570965988404*x`

So GT = `-3.39285482994202*x**3 - 6.78570965988404*x - 0.264836809498916*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) + 0.523287159969136*sin(t) - 0.710540944238196*Abs(v)**(1/3)`

The GT contains these basis functions/terms:
1. `x**3` (cubic in x)
2. `x` (linear in x)
3. `x * |v|^(1/3)` (cross term)
4. `sin(t)` 
5. `|v|^(1/3)` (cube root of absolute velocity)

Key features: The GT depends on `|v|^(1/3)`, which is a fractional power of |v|. This is NOT equivalent to `v^2`, `tanh(x)`, `x/(x^2+1)`, or any polynomial/rational function of v.

Let me now check each candidate:

**Candidates 1-5, 8-9, 11-18, 25-26:** These contain combinations of `x`, `x**3`, `sin(t)`, `tanh(x)`, `x/(x^2+1)` but **no dependence on v at all** (or only through constants that can be zeroed). The GT has essential `|v|^(1/3)` terms (`x*|v|^(1/3)` and `|v|^(1/3)`), which cannot be produced without v-dependent terms. These are all **NO MATCH**.

**Candidate 10:** Has `c9*v**3` - this is `v^3`, not `|v|^(1/3)`. Cannot match. **NO MATCH**.

**Candidate 12:** Same as above group, no v dependence. **NO MATCH**.

**Candidates 6-7, 20-24, 27-43:** These contain `v**2` terms and/or `exp(t)` terms. The GT requires `|v|^(1/3)` which is fundamentally different from `v^2`. No combination of `v^2` terms can produce `|v|^(1/3)`. Also, `exp(c*|t|)*cos(t)` cannot equal `sin(t)` for all t (different basis functions). **NO MATCH** for all.

**Candidate 19:** Has `c6*x*(c7 + v)**c8` - this could potentially give `x*|v|^(1/3)` if c7=0 and c8=1/3, but `(v)^(1/3)` ≠ `|v|^(1/3)` for negative v. Also missing standalone `|v|^(1/3)` term. **NO MATCH**.

**Candidates 44-50:** These contain `v**2*x`, `exp(t)*sin(x)`, `log(|v|+1)`, `cos(t)` etc. None can produce `|v|^(1/3)` terms. **NO MATCH**.

Let me verify my conclusion for all candidates - none of them contain `|v|^(1/3)` or `Abs(v)**(1/3)` as a basis function, which is essential in the GT and cannot be approximated by any of the offered functional forms.
